Lab Result (63) Schema Properties:


NON-FILEMAN CROSS REFERENCES


AP x-ref for certified/uncertified reports by location:
^LR("AC"_x_"L"_uc,LRREQLOC,LRPTN,LRIDT)=""
"x" = single letter AP acc. area (A=AU, B=BM, G=CG, N=CN, S=SP)
"uc" = "U" for uncertified or "C" for certified

Cancelled Orders
^LR("ACAN",LRWE,9999999-LRNOW,LRAAD,LRPTN,LRTST)=LRACC^DUZ^LRORT

Certified Accession x-ref
^LR("ACC",LRACC,LRPTN,LRIDT)=""

Accumulator x-ref
^LR("ACUM",LRREQLOC,LRPTN,LRSS,LRIDT,LRTST)=LRORT^LRHCP

Added a test to accession x-ref
^LR("ADD",LRWE,9999999-LRNOW,LRACC,LRPTN,LRTST,LROR)=LRACC^DUZ^
LRORT^LRNOW

Provider accumulative x-ref
^LR("AHCP",LRHCP,LRNOW,LRNAME^LRPTN,LRIDT)=""

Infection Control x-ref
^LR("AMIC",LRDIV,LRCDT,LRPTN,test)=LRIDT

Activity Master Log x-ref
^LR("AMLG",DT,LRNAME(25)^LRPTN,LRIDT,LRTCORD(5)^test)=LRORT^LRAA^LRMPR

Modified accession x-ref
^LR("AMOD",LRWE,LRIDT,LRAAD,LRPTN,LRTST)=LRACC^DUZ^LRORT^LROR

Uncertified accessions x-ref
^LR("APRPT",accession,LRPTN,LRIDT)=""

QNS Report x-ref
^LR("AQNS",DATE,LRAA,LRAN,TST)=LRPTN^DUZ^LRACP^LRORT^LRSS^LRIDT^
LROR^cert dt

Result Referral Report
^LR("AREF",LRDIV,LRMTF)=LRPRT^LRCDT
^LR("AREF",LRDIV,LRMTF,LRHCP,LRNAME^LRPTN,LRIDT,LRORT)=LRSS^LROR^
LRDT^LRCDT

Sensitive Result Referral Report
^LR("AREFS",LRDIV,LRMTF)=LRPRT^LRCDT
^LR("AREFS",LRDIV,LRMTF,LRHCP,LRNAME^LRPTN,LRIDT,LRORT)=LRSS^LROR^
LRDT^LRCDT

Sensitive Result Report (cume sort) x-ref
^LR("ASCS",LRDIV,TYPE,SC1,SC2,LRPTN,LRCORD,LRSS,LRIDT,TST)=cert dt

Batch HIV x-ref
^LR("ASRR",LRWE,certdt,SC,DC,LRNAME^LRPTN,LRTST,LRIDT)=LRORT^LRACC^LRMPR

Results performed by an outside lab that are pending local verification
^LR("AVRR",LRWE,date/time results received,LRPTN,LRSS,LRIDT,LROTST)=""

Where LROTST = order test ien


accession = abbreviation and number, EX: CHT 45 (no date)
cert dt = certify date, fileman format, day only
DATE = date, FileMan format
date-set = date FileMan format
DC = duty code ^DODT(8156,LRPC,8700) or 999999 if node is undefined
DT = date FileMan format
DUZ = user id number #3
LRAA = accession area pointer #68
LRAAD = accession area 2 or 3 letter abbreviation (CHT, HET, etc.)
LRACC = full accession name (901112 CHT 162)
LRACP = accession pointer #66
LRALERT = alert code (I=immediate results, S=sensitive, etc.)
LRAMEND = flag (=1) if result was amended
LRAN = accession number
LRCDT = certify date FileMan format
LRCORD = print order (might be LRSS if CUM printer order is undefined)
LRDIV = division #40.8 (and 69.91 for LAB info)
LRDT = Fileman date (no time) when printed
LRHCP = doctor pointer #6
LRHCPDUZ = user id for doctor #3
LRIDT = inverse collection date (9999999-collection date)
LRMPR = MEPRS code, pointer #8119
LRMTF = pointer to referring MTF #8101.1
LRNAME = patient name (first 25 characters)
LRNOW = date & time test added (FileMan format)
LROR = order pointer #101
LRORT = order task pointer #107
LRPC = $P(^DPT(LRPTN,8010),U,5)
LRPRT = Printed/Not Printed
LRPTN = patient pointer #2
LRREQLOC = requesting location pointer #44
LRSS = lab subscript, or type of test (CH,BT,SP,BM, etc)
LRTCORD = print order(5 numbers justified)
LRTST = ordered lab test, pointer #60
LRWE = lab work element pointer #69.92
SC = source code $P(^OR(orpt,110),U,9)
SC1 = sort criteria one, location pointer #44
SC2 = sort criteria two, patient name or terminal digits (last 4 digits
of SSN reversed. EX: 1234 reversed is 34^12)
test = process test, pointer to #60
TYPE = IN or OUT patient flag I=in, O=out

Special technical information regarding all fields that contain the
word LOINC in their field name. The acronym LOINC is for (L)ogical
(O)bservation (I)dentifiers, (N)ames, and (C)odes.

The various LOINC Code fields are the actual LOINC Code assigned by the
system for a test result. If the system can determine the LOINC code, it is
automatically assigned. For Clinical Chemistry tests, LOINC codes are
derived by the system based on the component name of the test, the
site/specimen for the accession, and lab method used during result entry.
The Lab Method contains the necessary references to determine the
appropriate LOINC Time Aspect, LOINC Property, LOINC System/Sample (which
is further linked via the Topography Field file), LOINC Scale, and
optionally LOINC Method. For Bacteriology accessions, a LOINC Code is
captured for the GRAM STAIN field (if this field is populated during result
entry), for each microorganism identified, and for each antibiotic tested.
For Autopsy, Bone Marrow, Cytology GYN, Cytology Non-GYN, and Surgical
Pathology accessions, a single LOINC code is assigned for each accession.
This LOINC code applies to all result entry fields for that accession. For
Mycology accessions, a LOINC code is captured for each Fungus/Yeast
identified. For Parasitology, a LOINC code is captured for each parasite
identified. For Mycobacterium, LOINC codes are captured for each
Mycobacterium identified and each antibiotic tested. For Virology, a LOINC
code is captured for each virus identified.

Tests in the BB (Blood Bank) subscript currently are not assigned LOINC
codes. CHCS is not considered the source of blood bank test results, the
DBSS (Defense Blood Standard System) is the source. LOINC Codes should be
derived on the system that is the source of the test results. At this time
(March 1999), the DBSS system and the HL-7 interface between CHCS and DBSS
does not support the exchange of LOINC codes for Blood Bank test results,
antibody identifications, or blood product management.

Data in these fields are actual LOINC code values determined by the system
for a particular test result. The data have the same values as the .01
field of the LOINC Codes file (file #8199). Note these fields are NOT
pointer fields. This is to allow test results and LOINC codes to be
assigned that may not be in the LOINC codes file. A LOINC code which is not
in CHCS may be captured from an off-board system via an HL-7 message when
the off-board system is using a different version of the LOINC tables.

Data in these fields should not be modified by the user and are generally
hidden from most data entry mechanisms. Only authorized support personnel
should change data in the LOINC code fields.

OrderLabelTypeDescription
1Patient (patient-63) POINTER (Patient-2)Pointer to the patient file
2Micro Conversion Flag (micro_conversion_flag-63) ENUMERATION This field was used internally to flag those micro results
that were converted from being stored in the '120' node to the
new micro structure that was determined for archive prior to 4.41.
If the conversion was done prior to 4.41, this field should contain a 1.
This field will be used again for 4.41 micro conversion.
The conversion routine looks at this field to determine whether the
conversion should be done for 4.41 or not. If this field does not contain
a 2, then the conversion will be done for the patient. After the conversion
is done on the patient, this field will be set to 2 to indicate that the
conversion was completed for this patient for 4.41
This field IS NOT TO BE EDITED!
Changing the status of this field could corrupt existing data!
 Micro result converted prior to 4.41; Micro result converted for 4.41
3Blood Bank (blood_bank-63) [OBJECT] This multiple contains the blood bank results received from the DBSS
interface. This data is owned and manipulated by the DBSS system; there are
no result entry screens associated with this subscript.
 
Subclass: Blood Bank (63_59)
OrderLabelTypeDescription
3.1Collection Date/Time (collection_date_time-63_59) DATE-TIMEThis field indicates the date and time a sample was collected.
3.2Accession Number (accession_number-63_59) STRINGThis field contains the number which identifies the specimen. Examples:
940926 BBA 1570, 940926 BBC 67. It is assigned when the specimen is
logged into the lab system.
3.3Requesting Location (requesting_location-63_59) POINTER (Hospital_Location-44)This field contains the area of the Medical Treatment Facility (e.g. clinic,
inpatient unit) where test request was ordered.
3.4Requesting Hcp (requesting_hcp-63_59) POINTER (Provider-6)This field contains the health care provider who ordered the test.
This is usually a physician.
3.5Collection Sample (collection_sample-63_59) POINTER (Collection_Sample-62)This field contains the type of material obtained from the patient. A
SPECIMEN is derived from a COLLECTION SAMPLE. Example: a COLLECTION
SAMPLE of blood may be split into SPECIMENS of serum or plasma.
3.6Log-In Date/Time (login_date_time-63_59) DATE-TIMEThis field stores the date/time a specimen is logged into the system. This
is collected automatically in the background. The user does not enter this
data.
3.7Lab Work Element (lab_work_element-63_59) POINTER (Hospital_Location-44)This field specifies the laboratory where the testing is performed.
3.8Lab Archive Date (lab_archive_date-63_59) DATE-TIMEThis field indicates the date that a lab entry is ready to be archived.
3.9Archived Flag (archived_flag-63_59) ENUMERATION This field indicates a '1' if the lab entry has been archived.
 ARCHIVED
3.10Accession Pointer (accession_pointer-63_59) POINTER (Accession-66)This field contains the internal entry number of the accession number
assigned to this specimen.
3.11Accession Status (accession_status-63_59) ENUMERATION This field indicates the current status of the accession. DBSS will
transmit only certified blood bank results to CHCS. Even though the
results are certified, the accession will have a status of Intermediate
until the last certified result and the last unit status is transmitted
to CHCS for this accession. At this time, the accession status will be
Final. Amending an individual blood bank test result will not change the
accession status to amended. The accession status will be Amended only if
a change is made to the unit status after the accession has a status of
Final.
 INTERMEDIATE; FINAL; AMENDED/UNIT STATUS UPDATED
3.12Origin Of Result (origin_of_result-63_59) ENUMERATION When this field is populated, it indicates that the accession was resulted
by an outside laboratory or non-CHCS system. The test(s) on this accession
are in the BB subscript.
 PERFORMING LABORATORY; COPATH; DBSS; OFFBOARD
3.13Result (result-63_59) [OBJECT] This multiple field contains the attributes for a Blood Bank Result.
 
Subclass: Result (63_794)
OrderLabelTypeDescription
3.13.1Lab Test Processed (lab_test_processed-63_794) IENThis field contains the name of the Blood Bank test performed.
3.13.2Result (result-63_794) STRINGThis field contains the answer to the test performed. The result field
is free text and contains the result transmitted from the DBSS. All test
results transmitted from DBSS to CHCS are certified. Results for only
certain single tests are stored in this multiple. These tests include
ABO/RH, Direct Antiglobulin, and Antibody Screen when the result is
negative. Results for positive Antibody Screen which includes Antibody ID
and/or Antibody Titer and results for unit status are stored in separate
multiples. A certify date and time must be specified for a user outside of
the lab to view the result.
3.13.3Certify Date/Time (certify_date_time-63_794) DATE-TIMEThis field indicates the date and time the result was certified. At this
point, the result becomes available to personnel and providers outside of
the laboratory.
3.13.4Certify Person (certify_person-63_794) POINTER (User-3)This field contains a generic certify person name. Because DBSS does
not maintain the CHCS USER file as a Master File, a generic DBSS,USER
will be used to populate this field. Refer to the DBSS for the actual
name of the user who certified the test.
3.13.5Result Status (result_status-63_794) ENUMERATION This field indicates the status of the blood bank test result. All blood
bank test results are certified when transmitted from DBSS to CHCS and will
have a status of Final. If a change is made to the certified result on DBSS,
the new result is flagged as an amendement and the result status is Amended.
 FINAL; AMENDED
3.13.6Initial Viewer Date/Time (initial_viewer_date_time-63_794) DATE-TIMEThis field stores the date/time a user first viewed the result.
3.13.7Initial Viewer (initial_viewer-63_794) POINTER (User-3)This field stores the internal entry number of the user who first looks
at the result via all result reporting options except the Daily Cumulative
and Interim reports. If the user is a lab user the field will not be set.
3.13.8Order Task (order_task-63_794) POINTER (Order_Task-107)This field stores the task number generated by Order Entry when the order
is created.
3.13.9Rnr Hcp (rnr_hcp-63_794) POINTER (Provider-6)This field stores the internal entry number of the Health Care Provider or
surrogate that printed, tossed, saved, or discarded a result in the
Review New Results option.
3.13.10Rnr Date/Time (rnr_date_time-63_794) DATE-TIMEThis field stores the date/time that the Health Care Provider or surrogate
tossed, printed, saved, or discarded the result in the Review New Results
option.
3.13.11Rnr Action (rnr_action-63_794) ENUMERATION If this field contains a "1", the Health Care Provider or surrogate
discarded the result without first viewing it in the Review New Results
option. This field will be set to "0" if the Health Care Provider or
surrogate tossed, saved, or printed the result in the Review New Results
option.
 INITIALED; DISCARDED
3.13.12Priority Result (priority_result-63_794) BOOLEANIf this field contains a "1", it indicates that the result was sent to the
Review New Results option and requesting location printer as a priority
result. Because the DBSS cannot flag individual blood bank results or
accessions as priority, all results transmitted from the DBSS will be
priority results.
3.13.13Appended/Amended Rnr (appended_amended_rnr-63_794) [OBJECT] This is the multiple that stores the ID and date/time of the Health Care
Provider that tossed, saved, printed, or discarded appended or amended
results in the Review New Results option.
 
Subclass: Appended/Amended Rnr (63_795)
OrderLabelTypeDescription
3.13.13.1Appended/Amended Rnr Hcp (appended_amended_rnr_hcp-63_795) POINTER (Provider-6)This field will store the ID of the Health Care Provider or surrogate that
printed, tossed, saved, or discarded an addendum result in Review New
Results option.
3.13.13.2Appended/Amended Rnr Date/Time (appended_amended_rnr_date_time-63_795) DATE-TIMEThis field will store the date/time the Health Care Provider or surrogate
printed, tossed, saved, or discarded an amended result in Review New
Results option.
3.13.13.3Appended/Amended Rnr Action (appended_amended_rnr_action-63_795) ENUMERATION This field contains a "1" if the Health Care Provider or surrogate discarded
the amended results without first viewing them in Review New Results option.
This field will be "0" if the Health Care Provider or surrogate tossed,
saved, or printed the result in Review New Results option.
 INITIALED; DISCARDED
3.13.14Antibody (antibody-63_794) [OBJECT] This multiple stores the antibodies identified from a positive antibody
screen result and the titer results associated with the antibodies. Each
antibody is stored as a separate entry.
 
Subclass: Antibody (63_796)
OrderLabelTypeDescription
3.13.14.1Antibody Id (antibody_id-63_796) STRINGThis field stores the result of a positive Antibody Screen test. Each
antibody identified from the antibody screen is stored as a separate
entry in the multiple.
3.13.14.2Antibody Titer (antibody_titer-63_796) STRINGThis field stores the antibody titer result that is associated with an
antibody identification from a positive Antibody Screen test. Each antibody
titer result is stored as a separate entry.
3.13.15Result History (result_history-63_794) [OBJECT] This multiple field contains the blood bank test result before it was
amended. When a blood bank test result is certified on DBSS, it is
transmitted to CHCS. If the certified result is changed on DBSS, it is
considered amended on CHCS. The previous certified result will be filed in
the result history field.
 
Subclass: Result History (63_797)
OrderLabelTypeDescription
3.13.15.1Date/Time Result Changed (date_time_result_changed-63_797) DATE-TIMEThis field contains the date and time that a result was changed
on DBSS.
3.13.15.2Result (result-63_797) STRINGThis field contains the previously reported certified result for a blood
bank test before the result was amended on DBSS. Test results are always
certifed when transmitted from DBSS to CHCS. When a certified result is
changed on DBSS, the new result and its associated required comment are
filed as amended results in the result field on CHCS. The previously
reported result is stored in this multiple for audit purposes. The result
field is free text and contains the result transmitted from DBSS. A certify
date and time must be specified for a user outside of the lab to view the
result.
3.13.15.3Certify Date/Time (certify_date_time-63_797) DATE-TIMEThis field indicates the date and time the amended result was certified
on DBSS. At this point, the result becomes available to personnel and
providers outside of the laboratory.
3.13.15.4Certify Person (certify_person-63_797) POINTER (User-3)This field contains a generic certify person name. Because DBSS
does not maintain the CHCS USER file as a Master File, a generic
DBSS,USER will be used to populate this field. Refer to the DBSS
for the actual name of the user who certified the amended result.
3.13.15.5Initial Viewer Date/Time (initial_viewer_date_time-63_797) DATE-TIMEThis field stores the date/time a user first viewed the result.
3.13.15.6Initial Viewer (initial_viewer-63_797) POINTER (User-3)Ths field stores the internal entry number of the user who first looks at
the result via all result reporting options except the Daily Cumulative
and Interim reports. If the user is a lab user, the field will not be set.
3.13.15.7Rnr Hcp (rnr_hcp-63_797) POINTER (Provider-6)This field stores the internal entry number of the Health Care Provider or
surrogate that printed, tossed, saved, or discarded a result in the Review
New Results option.
3.13.15.8Rnr Date/Time (rnr_date_time-63_797) DATE-TIMEThis field stores the date/time that the Health Care Provide or surrogate
tossed, printed, saved, or discarded the result in the Review New Results
option.
3.13.15.9Rnr Action (rnr_action-63_797) ENUMERATION If this field contains a "1", the Health Care Provider or surrogate
discarded the result without first viewing it in the Review New Results
option. This field will be set to "0" if the Health Care Provider or
surrogate tossed, saved, or printed the result in the Review New Results
option.
 INITIALED; DISCARDED
3.13.15.10Antibody (antibody-63_797) [OBJECT] This multiple stores the antibodies identified from a positive antibody
screen result and the titer results associated with the antibody before
it was amended. Each antibody is stored as a separate entry.
 
Subclass: Antibody (63_798)
OrderLabelTypeDescription
3.13.15.10.1Antibody Id (antibody_id-63_798) STRINGThis field stores the result of a positive Antibody Screen test before it
was amended. Test results are always certified when transmitted from DBSS
to CHCS. When a certified result is changed on DBSS, the new result and
its associated required comment are filed as amended results in the
Antibody ID field. The previously reported Antibody ID result is stored
in this multiple for audit purposes.
3.13.15.10.2Antibody Titer (antibody_titer-63_798) STRINGThis field stores the antibody titer result that is associated with an
antibody identification from a positive Antibody Screen test before it was
amended. Test results are always certified when transmitted from DBSS to
CHCS. When a certified result is changed on DBSS, the new result and its
associated required comment are filed as amended results in the Antibody
Titer field. The previously reported antibody titer result is stored in
this field for audit purposes.
3.13.15.11Result Comment (result_comment-63_797) STRINGThis field is free text and contains a comment entered on DBSS
when a certified result has been changed on DBSS. The result
comment is required and is transmitted to CHCS with the new
result. This field will only contain an entry if the result has
been amended on DBSS.
3.13.16Result Comment (result_comment-63_794) STRINGThis field is free text and contains a comment entered on DBSS when
a certified result has been changed on DBSS. The result comment is
required and is transmitted to CHCS with the new result. This field
will only contain an entry if the result has been amended on DBSS.
3.13.17Performing Lab Disclosure (performing_lab_disclosure-63_794) NUMERICThis field contains the identifier linking the resulted test to the disclosure
statement received from the performing laboratory. This field is maintained
by the Lab Interoperability interface. DO NOT EDIT THIS FIELD.
3.14Unit Status (unit_status-63_59) [OBJECT] This multiple field contains the blood products associated with an order
for crossmatching or autologous donation and the current status of unit
availability.
 
Subclass: Unit Status (63_799)
OrderLabelTypeDescription
3.14.1Blood Product Type (blood_product_type-63_799) POINTER (Blood_Product_Type-8161)This field contains the blood product requested for crossmatching or for
collection by autologous donation.
3.14.2Number Of Units Ordered (number_of_units_ordered-63_799) NUMERICThis field contains the number of units of a blood product type requested
for crossmatching or for collection in an Autologous Donation order.
3.14.3Date/Time Units Collected (date_time_units_collected-63_799) DATE-TIMEThis field contains the collection date and time of the most recent unit
collected for an Autologous Donation order.
3.14.4Number Of Units Collected (number_of_units_collected-63_799) NUMERICThis field contains the number of units specified in an Autologous
Donation order which have been collected.
3.14.5Unit Status Date/Time (unit_status_date_time-63_799) DATE-TIMEThis field contains the date/time that DBSS updated the number of units
available, issued, or transfused for a crossmatched blood product. It is
the date/time that DBSS performed the update and not the date/time CHCS
received the update.
3.14.6Number Of Units Available (number_of_units_available-63_799) NUMERICThis field contains the current number of units from a Type and Crossmatch
order that have been crossmatched and are ready for issue to the patient.
3.14.7Number Of Units Issued (number_of_units_issued-63_799) NUMERICThis field contains the current number of units from a Type and Crossmatch
order which have been signed out to the patient.
3.14.8Number Of Units Transfused (number_of_units_transfused-63_799) NUMERICThis field contains the current number of units from a Type and Crossmatch
order which have been transfused to the patient.
3.14.9Unit Status History (unit_status_history-63_799) [OBJECT] This multiple field contains an audit trail of updates made to any of the
unit status fields. When the first unit status is filed on CHCS, it will be
filed into the Unit Status field. DBSS will transmit any change in unit
status to CHCS. The current unit status will file in the Unit Status field,
and the previous unit status result will be moved into the Unit Status
History fields. Both the current Unit Status and the Unit Status History
will display in CHCS inquiry and reporting options.
 
Subclass: Unit Status History (63_8)
OrderLabelTypeDescription
3.14.9.1Date/Time Product Updated (date_time_product_updated-63_8) DATE-TIMEThis field contains the date and time of the previously reported unit
status before an update was filed. Each time a unit status changes,
the time it was completed on DBSS is captured and displayed on CHCS to
reflect current unit availability.
3.14.9.2Date/Time Units Collected (date_time_units_collected-63_8) DATE-TIMEThis field contains the collection date and time of the most recent unit
collection date and time for an Autologous Donation order before an update
was filed.
3.14.9.3Number Of Units Collected (number_of_units_collected-63_8) NUMERICThis field contains the number of units collected in an Autologous
Donation order which were previously reported before an update was filed.
3.14.9.4Accession Status (accession_status-63_8) ENUMERATION This field contains the actual status for this accession when DBSS sends an
update to the unit status information. This allows CHCS to appropriately
note that the unit status data was updated by DBSS while the accession
was either intermediate or finalized. Each unit status update that is
transmitted after the accession is finalized is considered an amendment
by CHCS.
 INTERMEDIATE; FINAL; AMENDED/UNIT STATUS UPDATED
3.14.9.5Number Of Units Available (number_of_units_available-63_8) NUMERICThis field contains the number of units from a Type and Crossmatch order
that was previously reported as crossmatched and ready for issue before
an update was made to the unit status.
3.14.9.6Number Of Units Issued (number_of_units_issued-63_8) NUMERICThis field contains the number of units from a Type and Crossmatch order
that was previously reported as signed out to the patient before an update
was made to the unit status.
3.14.9.7Number Of Units Transfused (number_of_units_transfused-63_8) NUMERICThis field contains the number of units from a Type and Crossmatch order
that was previously reported as transfused to the patient before an update
was made to the unit status.
3.15Performing Lab Disclosures (performing_lab_disclosures-63_59) [OBJECT] This multiple field contains the disclosure statements received from the
performing laboratory. Each entry in this multiple field is associated with
one or more resulted tests on the accession. This field is maintained by the
Lab Interoperability interface. DO NOT EDIT THIS FIELD.
 
Subclass: Performing Lab Disclosures (63_763)
OrderLabelTypeDescription
3.15.1Disclosure Id (disclosure_id-63_763) NUMERICThis field contains a unique identifier for the disclosure text received from
the performing laboratory. This field is maintained by the Lab
Interoperability interface. DO NOT EDIT THIS FIELD.
3.15.2Disclosure Text (disclosure_text-63_763) STRINGThis field contains the disclosure statement received from the performing
laboratory. It identifies the facility that performed the test. This field
is maintained by the Lab Interoperability interface. DO NOT EDIT THIS FIELD.
4Clinical Chemistry (clinical_chemistry-63) [OBJECT] This multiple contains the attributes of Clinical
Chemistry results. These results are free text,
numeric, or set of codes for the Lab Sections of
Chemistry, Hematology, Coagulation, or Serology.
 
Subclass: Clinical Chemistry (63_04)
OrderLabelTypeDescription
4.1Date/Time Specimen Taken (date_time_specimen_taken-63_04) DATE-TIMEThis field indicates the date and time a specimen was collected.
4.2Accession (accession-63_04) STRINGThis field contains the number which identifies a specimen.
Examples: 940926 CHC 1570, 940926 CHA 67. It is assigned
when the specimen is logged into the lab system.
4.3Specimen (specimen-63_04) POINTER (Topography_Field-61)This field indicates the type of material to be tested.
Examples: Serum, plasma, urine.
4.4Requesting Location (requesting_location-63_04) POINTER (Hospital_Location-44)Area of Medical Treatment Facility (e.g. clinic,
inpatient unit) where test request was ordered.
4.5Hcp (hcp-63_04) POINTER (Provider-6)Health care provider who ordered the test.
This is usually a physician.
4.6Collection Sample (collection_sample-63_04) POINTER (Collection_Sample-62)This field contains the type of material obtained
from the patient. A SPECIMEN is derived from a
COLLECTION SAMPLE. Example: A COLLECTION SAMPLE
of blood may be split into SPECIMENS of serum or plasma.
4.7Log-In Date/Time (login_date_time-63_04) DATE-TIMEThis field stores the date/time a specimen is logged
into the system. This is collected automatically in
the background. The user does not enter this data.
4.8Lab Work Element (lab_work_element-63_04) POINTER (Hospital_Location-44)This field specifies the laboratory where the testing
is performed.
4.9Lab Archive Date (lab_archive_date-63_04) DATE-TIMEThis field indicates the date that a lab entry is ready to
be archived.
4.10Archived Flag (archived_flag-63_04) ENUMERATION This field contains a "1" if the lab entry has been archived.
 ARCHIVED
4.11Origin Of Result (origin_of_result-63_04) ENUMERATION When this field is populated, it indicates that the accession was resulted
by an outside laboratory or non-CHCS system. The test(s) on this accession
are in the CH subscript.
 PERFORMING LABORATORY; COPATH; DBSS; OFFBOARD
4.12Result (result-63_04) [OBJECT] This multiple field contains the attributes
for a Clinical Chemistry result.
 
Subclass: Result (63_07)
OrderLabelTypeDescription
4.12.1Test (test-63_07) IENThis field contains the name of the Clinical
Chemistry test performed.
4.12.2Result (result-63_07) STRINGThis field contains the answer to the test performed.
The result can be text or numeric. An "@" sign
indicates a sensitive result. A "set of codes" result
is as defined in the Lab Method file. A certify date
and time must be specified for a user outside of the
lab to view the result.
4.12.3Sensitive Result (sensitive_result-63_07) STRINGThis field contains the result for a test designated
as sensitive. Only the requesting Health Care Provider
assigned the LRSENSITIVE security key may view this result.
4.12.4Rnr Hcp (rnr_hcp-63_07) POINTER (Provider-6)This field will store the ID of the Health Care Provider
or surrogate that printed, tossed, saved, or discarded
a result in Review New Results option.
4.12.5Rnr Date/Time (rnr_date_time-63_07) DATE-TIMEThis field stores the date/time that the Health Care
Provider or surrogate tossed, printed, saved, or
discarded a result in Review New Results option.
4.12.6Rnr Action (rnr_action-63_07) ENUMERATION If this field contains a "1", the Health Care Provider
or surrogate discarded the result without first viewing
in Review New Results option. This field will be set
"0" if the Health Care Provider or surrogate tossed,
saved, or printed the result in Review New Results option.
 INITIALED; DISCARDED
4.12.7Lab Method (lab_method-63_07) POINTER (Lab_Method-8710)This field indicates what lab method was used to perform this
test at the time it was resulted. Example: Enzymes tests
performed by a procedure using different temperatures.
4.12.8Cpt/Amt Workload Flag (cpt_amt_workload_flag-63_07) BOOLEANIf this field is set to "YES", that indicates that this test is an
Automated Multichannel test and has already been included in the
workload calculation.
4.12.9Auto Instrument (auto_instrument-63_07) POINTER (Auto_Instrument-62_4)This field contains the name of the auto instrument used to create
this result.
4.12.10Priority Result (priority_result-63_07) BOOLEANIf this field contains a "1", it indicates that the
result was sent to the Review New Results option and
requesting location printer as a priority result.
4.12.11Clinical Chemistry Loinc Code (clinical_chemistry_loinc_code-63_07) STRINGThis field is the LOINC Code assigned by the system for this test result.
If the system can determine the LOINC code, it is automatically assigned.
For Clinical Chemistry tests, LOINC codes are derived by the system based
on the component name of the test, the site/specimen for the accession, and
lab method used during result entry. The Lab Method contains the necessary
references to determine the appropriate LOINC Time Aspect, LOINC Property,
LOINC System/Sample (which is further linked via the Topography Field
file), LOINC Scale, and optionally LOINC Method.

Data in this field is the actual LOINC code value determined for this test.
The data is the same as the .01 field of the LOINC Codes file (file #8199).
Note this field is NOT a pointer field. This is to allow test results and
LOINC codes to be assigned that may not be in the LOINC codes file. A LOINC
code which is not in CHCS may be captured from an off-board system via an
HL-7 message when the off-board system is using a different version of the
LOINC tables.

Data in this field should not be modified by the user and is generally
hidden from most data entry mechanisms.
4.12.12Alert (alert-63_07) STRINGThis field stores designations for abnormal results.
Examples: "H", "L", "H*", "L*".
4.12.13Appended/Amended Rnr (appended_amended_rnr-63_07) [OBJECT] This is the multiple that stores the ID and date/time
of the Health Care Provider that tossed, saved, printed,
or discarded appended or amended results in Review New
Results option.
 
Subclass: Appended/Amended Rnr (63_775)
OrderLabelTypeDescription
4.12.13.1Appended/Amended Rnr Hcp (appended_amended_rnr_hcp-63_775) POINTER (Provider-6)This field will store the ID of the Health Care Provider
or surrogate that printed, tossed, saved, or discarded
an addendum result in Review New Results option.
4.12.13.2Appended/Amended Rnr Date/Time (appended_amended_rnr_date_time-63_775) DATE-TIMEThis field will store the date/time the Health Care
Provider or surrogate printed, tossed, saved, or
discarded an amended result in Review New Results
option.
4.12.13.3Appended/Amended Rnr Action (appended_amended_rnr_action-63_775) ENUMERATION This field contains a "1" if the Health Care Provider
or surrogate discarded the amended results without
first viewing them in Review New Results option.
This field will be "0" if the Health Care Provider or
surrogate tossed, saved, or printed the result in
Review New Results option.
 INITIALED; DISCARDED
4.12.14Enter Date/Time (enter_date_time-63_07) DATE-TIMEThis field contains the date and time the result was entered
and filed. Only lab users will see the result at this point,
as it is filed but not certified.
4.12.15Enter Person (enter_person-63_07) POINTER (User-3)This field indicates the person who entered and filed
the result. It may or may not be the same user that
certifies the result. Only lab users will see the result
at this point, because it is filed but not certified.
4.12.16Certify Date/Time (certify_date_time-63_07) DATE-TIMEThis field indicates the date and time the result was
certified. At this point, the result becomes available
to personnel and providers outside of the laboratory.
4.12.17Certify Person (certify_person-63_07) POINTER (User-3)This field indicates the person who certified the result.
At this point, the result becomes available to personnel
and providers outside of the laboratory.
4.12.18Exclude Value (exclude_value-63_07) BOOLEANThis field is used to exclude result from statistical
(quality control) calculations.
4.12.19Exclusion Comment (exclusion_comment-63_07) STRINGThis field is used to store a reason of exclusion for this
result from statistical (quality control) calculations.
4.12.20Initial Viewer Date/Time (initial_viewer_date_time-63_07) DATE-TIMEThis field stores the date/time a user first viewed the result.
4.12.21Initial Viewer (initial_viewer-63_07) POINTER (User-3)This field stores the ID of the user who first looks at the
result via all result reporting options except the Daily
Cumulative or Interim reports. If the user is a lab user
the field will not be set.
4.12.22Comment (comment-63_07) STRINGThis is a word processing field that allows the user to make
any comments during result entry. An example would be to note
if a specimen were hemolyzed.
4.12.23Order Task (order_task-63_07) POINTER (Order_Task-107)This field stores a task number generated by Order Entry when
the order is created.
4.12.24Secondary Order Indicator (secondary_order_indicator-63_07) POINTER (Lab_Test-60)This field is used to indicate that a secondary order has been
placed as defined by the laboratory.
4.12.25Delta Check (delta_check-63_07) STRINGThis field stores a previous numeric result which is used
for a delta check on the current numeric result for the
same test.
4.12.26Sensitive Alert (sensitive_alert-63_07) STRINGThis field stores designations for abnormal sensitive
results. Examples: "H", "L", "H*", "L*".
4.12.27Archive Interpretation (archive_interpretation-63_07) STRINGDO NOT ENTER DATA INTO THIS FIELD!!!!! This field is only
to be used internally by lab archive software during an
archive run. This field will NOT BE POPULATED with data
while a lab result is online (not archived). If data is
mistakenly entered into this field before a result is archived,
that data will be overwritten during an archive run.
4.12.28Units (units-63_07) STRINGThis field is the Units sent by the performing lab and will be used when
reporting this result.
4.12.29Normal Range (normal_range-63_07) STRINGThis field is the Normal Range sent by the performing lab and will be
used when reporting this result.
4.12.30Alert (alert-63_07-20_03) STRINGThis field is the Alert sent by the performing lab and will be used when
reporting this result.
4.12.31Interpretation (interpretation-63_07) STRINGThis field contains result comments received from the performing laboratory.
It is not used when a test is resulted at the originating lab.
4.12.32Performing Lab Disclosure (performing_lab_disclosure-63_07) NUMERICThis field contains the identifier linking the resulted test to the disclosure
statement received from the performing laboratory. This field is maintained
by the Lab Interoperability interface. DO NOT EDIT THIS FIELD.
4.13Panel With Duplicate Test (panel_with_duplicate_test-63_04) [OBJECT] This is a multiple field which stores attributes for a panel

Example: A Chem 7 panel which contains a glucose that has also

If the system can determine the LOINC code, it is automatically assigned.
For Bacteriology accessions, a LOINC Code is captured for the GRAM STAIN
field (if this field is populated during result entry), for each
microorganism identified, and for each antibiotic tested. Data in this
field is the actual LOINC code value determined for this test. The data is
the same as the .01 field of the LOINC Codes file (file #8199). Note this
field is NOT a pointer field. This is to allow test results and LOINC codes
to be assigned that may not be in the LOINC codes file. A LOINC code which
is not in CHCS may be captured from an off-board system via an HL-7 message
when the off-board system is using a different version of the LOINC tables.

Data in this field should not be modified by the user and is generally
hidden from most data entry mechanisms.
6.10.16.6Bt Org Snomed Ct (bt_org_snomed_ct-63_788) STRINGThis field contains the SNOMED CT code generated from the Etiology file and
received through the Lab Interoperability interface.

7Mycobacterium Buffer (mycobacterium_buffer-63) [OBJECT] This is a multiple field which contains attributes

OrderLabelTypeDescription
7.1Date/Time Specimen Taken (date_time_specimen_taken-63_16) DATE-TIMEThis field indicates the date and time a specimen was collected.
7.2Accession (accession-63_16) STRINGThis field contains the number which identifies a specimen.
Examples: 940926 MIA 1570, 940926 CHA 67. It is assigned
when the specimen is logged into the lab system.
7.3Specimen (specimen-63_16) POINTER (Topography_Field-61)This field indicates the type of material to be tested.
Examples: Stool, urine, sputum.
7.4Requesting Location (requesting_location-63_16) POINTER (Hospital_Location-44)Area of Medical Treatment Facility (e.g. clinic,
inpatient unit) where test request was ordered.
7.5Hcp (hcp-63_16) POINTER (Provider-6)Health care provider who ordered the test.

from the patient. A SPECIMEN is derived from a
COLLECTION SAMPLE. Example: A COLLECTION SAMPLE
could be an abscess or swab with the Specimen field
indicating the site of collection. The COLLECTION
SAMPLE might be urine or blood.
7.7Log-In Date/Time (login_date_time-63_16) DATE-TIMEThis field stores the date/time a specimen is logged
into the system. This is collected automatically in
the background. The user does not enter this data.
7.8Lab Work Element (lab_work_element-63_16) POINTER (Hospital_Location-44)This field specifies the laboratory where the testing is performed.
7.9Origin Of Result (origin_of_result-63_16) ENUMERATION When this field is populated, it indicates that the accession was resulted
by an outside laboratory or non-CHCS system. The test(s) on this accession
are in the TBBUFF subscript.
 PERFORMING LABORATORY; COPATH; DBSS; OFFBOARD
7.10Test (test-63_16) [OBJECT] This is a multiple field which contains attributes

Subclass: Test (63_17)
OrderLabelTypeDescription
7.10.1Test (test-63_17) POINTER (Lab_Test-60)This field contains the name of the test performed.
7.10.2Priority Result (priority_result-63_17) BOOLEANIf this field contains a "1", it indicates that the
result was sent to the Review New Results option
and requesting location printer as a priority result.
7.10.3Acid Fast Stain Loinc Code (acid_fast_stain_loinc_code-63_17) STRINGThis field is the LOINC Code assigned by the system for this test result. If

Mycobacterium accessions, a LOINC code is captured for each Mycobacterium TB

Data in this field should not be modified by the user and is generally hidden
from most data entry mechanisms.
7.10.4Result Type (result_type-63_17) ENUMERATION This field contains a set of internally stored codes
for indicating whether the results are INTERMEDIATE,
FINAL, or AMENDED. An intermediate result can be
certified. Once certified, the intermediate result
is not changed but the user may add additional results
until the result type is final.
 INTERMEDIATE; FINAL; INTERMEDIATE REPORT-PRIORITY; FINAL REPORT-PRIORITY; AMENDED FINAL REPORT
7.10.5Tb Result (tb_result-63_17) STRINGThis is a word processing field for entering TB results.

the user to enter acid-fast stain results.
Example: 3+ acid-fast bacteria.
7.10.7Enter Date/Time (enter_date_time-63_17) DATE-TIMEThis field contains the date and time the result was entered
and filed. Only lab users will see the result at this point,
as it is filed but not certified.
7.10.8Enter Person (enter_person-63_17) POINTER (User-3)This field indicates the person who entered and filed the
result. It may or may not be the same user that certifies
the result. Only lab users will see the result at this
point, as it is filed but not certified.
7.10.9Certify Date/Time (certify_date_time-63_17) DATE-TIMEThis field indicates the date and time the result was
certified. At this point, the result becomes available
to personnel and providers outside of the laboratory.
7.10.10Certify Person (certify_person-63_17) POINTER (User-3)This field indicates the person who certified the result.
At this point, the result becomes available to personnel
and providers outside the laboratory.

with the specimen. This number is generated by Order
Entry when the order is created.
7.10.12Mycobacterium Tb (mycobacterium_tb-63_17) [OBJECT] This field contains the name of the Mycobacterium identified. It points

Mycobacteria for a result. If a Mycobacterium is not available, then have
the lab manager check the Etiology Field file for the entry. If the entry
exists in the file, then identifier must be a Mycobacterium. If the entry is
not in the file, the lab manager may add it. Make sure the identifier is
a Mycobacterium.

9.10.1Test (test-63_29) POINTER (Lab_Test-60)This field contains the name of the test performed.
9.10.2Priority Result (priority_result-63_29) BOOLEANIf this field contains a "1", it indicates that the
result was sent to the Review New Results option
and requesting location printer as a priority result.
9.10.3Result Type (result_type-63_29) ENUMERATION This field contains a set of internally stored codes
for indicating whether the results are INTERMEDIATE,
FINAL, or AMENDED. An intermediate result can be
certified. Once certified, the intermediate result
is not changed but the user may add additional results
until the result type is final.
 INTERMEDIATE; FINAL; INTERMEDIATE REPORT-PRIORITY; FINAL REPORT-PRIORITY; AMENDED FINAL REPORT
9.10.4Virology Result (virology_result-63_29) STRINGThis is a word processing field used to enter
a Virology result.
9.10.5Virus (virus-63_29) [OBJECT] This is a multiple field which contains the attributes
to identify a virus. It points to the Etiology Field
file and has a screen so the user can only select a
Virus for a result. If a Virus is not available, then
have the lab manager check the Etilogy Field file for
the entry. If the entry exists in the file, the
identifier must be a virus. If the entry is not included
in the file, the lab manager may add it. Make sure the
identifier is a Virus.
 
Subclass: Virus (63_31)
OrderLabelTypeDescription
9.10.5.1Virus (virus-63_31) POINTER (Etiology_Field-61_2)This field contains the name of the virus identified.
It points to the Etilogy Field file and has a screen
so the user can only select a Virus for a result. If
a Virus is not available, then have the lab manager
check the Etilogy Field file for the entry. If the
entry exists in the file, the identifier must be a
Virus. If the entry is not included in the file, the
lab manager may add it. Make sure the identifier is
a Virus.
9.10.5.2Quantity (quantity-63_31) STRINGThis field is used to quantify the amount of virus
isolated. Examples: 1+, 2+, 3+.
9.10.5.3Virus Loinc Code (virus_loinc_code-63_31) STRINGThis field is the LOINC Code assigned by the system for this test result.
If the system can determine the LOINC code, it is automatically assigned.
For Virology, a LOINC code is captured for each virus identified.

Data in this field is the actual LOINC code value determined for this test.
The data is the same as the .01 field of the LOINC Codes file (file #8199).
Note this field is NOT a pointer field. This is to allow test results and
LOINC codes to be assigned that may not be in the LOINC codes file. A LOINC
code which is not in CHCS may be captured from an off-board system via an
HL-7 message when the off-board system is using a different version of the
LOINC tables.

Data in this field should not be modified by the user and is generally
hidden from most data entry mechanisms.
9.10.5.4Virus Snomed Ct (virus_snomed_ct-63_31) STRINGThis field contains the SNOMED CT code generated from the SNOMED encoding
process or received through the HL7 interface.
9.10.6Enter Date/Time (enter_date_time-63_29) DATE-TIMEThis field contains the date and time the result was entered
and filed. Only lab users will see the result at this point,
as it is filed but not certified.
9.10.7Enter Person (enter_person-63_29) POINTER (User-3)This field indicates the person who entered and filed the
result. It may or may not be the same user that certifies
the result. Only lab users will see the result at this
point, as it is filed but not certified.
9.10.8Certify Date/Time (certify_date_time-63_29) DATE-TIMEThis field indicates the date and time the result was
certified. At this point, the result becomes available
to personnel and providers outside of the laboratory.
9.10.9Certify Person (certify_person-63_29) POINTER (User-3)This field indicates the person who certified the result.
At this point, the result becomes available to personnel
and providers outside the laboratory.
9.10.10Order Task (order_task-63_29) POINTER (Order_Task-107)This field contains the order task number associated
with the specimen. This number is generated by Order
Entry when the order is created.
9.10.11Result Comment (result_comment-63_29) STRINGThis field is used to store result comments for send out tests.
9.10.12Performing Lab Disclosure (performing_lab_disclosure-63_29) NUMERICThis field contains the identifier linking the resulted test to the disclosure
statement received from the performing laboratory. This field is maintained
by the Lab Interoperability interface. DO NOT EDIT THIS FIELD.
9.11Panel With Duplicate Test (panel_with_duplicate_test-63_27) [OBJECT] This is a multiple field which stores attributes for a
panel containing a test which has been identified as a
duplicate order on the same accession number. Example:
A Chem 7 panel that contains a glucose which has also
been ordered as a separate glucose on the same accession.
 
Subclass: Panel With Duplicate Test (63_51)
OrderLabelTypeDescription

accession number. Example: A Chem 7 panel which
contains a glucose that has also been ordered as a
separate glucose on the same accession.
9.11.2Duplicate Test (duplicate_test-63_51) POINTERThis is a multiple field which contains the attributes
to identify a test as a duplicate if the test is also
part of another panel on the same accession. Example:
A separate glucose that has also been ordered on the
same accession as part of a Chem 7 panel.
9.12Performing Lab Disclosures (performing_lab_disclosures-63_27) [OBJECT] This multiple field contains the disclosure statements received from the

one or more resulted tests on the accession. This field is maintained by the
Lab Interoperability interface. DO NOT EDIT THIS FIELD.

11Surgical Pathology (surgical_pathology-63) [OBJECT] This is the area within Anatomic Pathology that deals with the

EXAMINATION. Also included under this area are frozen
sections. If a specimen is FROZEN it is prompted during the
Order Entry process.

12.37Requesting Hcp (requesting_hcp-63_44) POINTER (Provider-6)Enter the name of the Health Care Provider who requested the test.
12.38Log-In Comments (login_comments-63_44) STRINGThis is a free text file (up to 78 characters) that allows the user to
make any comments on the specimen during the log-in process. An example
of this would be if the specimen submitted was not properly fixed.
12.39Diagnosis (diagnosis-63_44) STRINGThis is a word processing field used to enter the
diagnosis associated with the Cyto-Gyn specimen.
12.40Diagnosis Comments (diagnosis_comments-63_44) STRINGThis is a free-text field (up to 78 characters)
that allows the user to make any comments relating
to the diagnosis.
12.41Other Findings (other_findings-63_44) STRINGThis is a word processing field used to enter any
other findings associated with this patient that
are relevant to this case.
12.42Estrogen Effect (estrogen_effect-63_44) ENUMERATION Maturing of squamous cells as seen on Pap smear. Estrogen
may be either natural or supplemental.
 ATROPHIC; LOW; MODERATE; MARKED
12.43Maturation Index (maturation_index-63_44) BOOLEANEnter YES if a maturation index is required. Enter NO or leave blank
if not required.
12.44Superficial (superficial-63_44) NUMERICEnter a number from 0 to 100 for the percent of SUPERFICIAL
( most mature squamous cells) seen on a Pap smear.
12.45Intermediate (intermediate-63_44) NUMERICEnter a number from 0 to 100 for the percent of INTERMEDIATE
(middle growing layer of squamous cells) seen on a Pap smear.
12.46Parabasal (parabasal-63_44) NUMERICEnter a number between 0 and 100 for the percent of PARABASAL
(reserve layer of squamous cells) seen on a Pap smear.
12.47Estrogen Invalid Due To (estrogen_invalid_due_to-63_44) STRINGThis is a free-text file (up to 78 characters) that allows the user to
make any comments on the examination of a Pap smear. For example,
estimation of estrogen effect may be invalid due to prevailing conditions
such as inflammation or other problem.
12.48Recommendations (recommendations-63_44) STRINGThis is a word processing field which allows the user
to enter a recommendation for a repeat examination
based on the diagnosis.
12.49Pathologist (pathologist-63_44) POINTER (Provider-6)This is the name of the pathologist responsible for signing out this case.
12.50Resident Pathologist (resident_pathologist-63_44) POINTER (Provider-6)Enter the name of the resident pathologist performing the tissue
examination.
12.51Cytotechnologist (cytotechnologist-63_44) POINTER (User-3)Enter the name of the cytotechnologist who prepared/screened
the Pap smear or other tissue slide(s).
12.52Reviewer (reviewer-63_44) POINTER (User-3)The name of the person who reviewed the case and |TAB|
entered QC results.
12.53Quality Control (quality_control-63_44) ENUMERATION This field contains the results of the QC review
of the Cytology-Gyn exam.
 AGREE; OVERCALL; UNDERCALL
12.54Status (status-63_44) ENUMERATION This field indicates the state of the result.
Options are filed, certified, and amended.
 CERTIFY; FILE; AMEND
12.55Certify Date/Time (certify_date_time-63_44) DATE-TIMEThis field contains the date/time the Cytology-Gyn
result was certified.
12.56Order Reference (order_reference-63_44) POINTER (Order-101)This field contains the order number associated with the specimen.
12.57Order Task (order_task-63_44) POINTER (Order_Task-107)This field contains the order task number associated
with the specimen. This number is generated by Order
Entry when the order is created.
12.58Certify Person (certify_person-63_44) POINTER (User-3)This field contains the user ID of the person
who certified the results.
12.598702 Pointer (_8702_pointer-63_44) POINTER (Sp_Accession_File-8702)This field links this patient's report to
the Surgical Pathology Accession File.
12.60Snomed (snomed-63_44) STRINGThis multiple contains the SNOMED codes generated
from the encoder or manually entered. SMOMED means
Systemized Nomenclature of Medicine. This is the
standardized description of the diagnosis.
12.61Ap Report (ap_report-63_44) STRINGThis field contains the result report text as formatted by a performing
laboratory or CoPath COTS system. DO NOT EDIT THIS FIELD!
12.62Result Comment (result_comment-63_44) STRINGThis field is used to store result comments for send out tests.
12.63Disclosure Statement (disclosure_statement-63_44) STRINGThis word processing field contains the disclosure statement as transmitted
by the performing laboratory.

certified the result.

13.22Typist (typist-63_46) STRINGThis field contains the name of the person who typed the report.
13.23Priority Result (priority_result-63_46) BOOLEANIf this field contains a "1", it indicates that the
result was sent to the Review New Results option
and requesting location printer as a priority result.
13.24Autopsy Loinc Code (autopsy_loinc_code-63_46) STRINGThis field is the LOINC Code assigned by the system for this test result.
If the system can determine the LOINC code, it is automatically assigned.
For Autopsy accessions, a single LOINC code is assigned for each accession.
This LOINC code applies to all result entry fields for that accession. Data
in this field is the actual LOINC code value determined for this test. The
data is the same as the .01 field of the LOINC Codes file (file #8199).
Note this field is NOT a pointer field. This is to allow test results and
LOINC codes to be assigned that may not be in the LOINC codes file. A LOINC
code which is not in CHCS may be captured from an off-board system via an
HL-7 message when the off-board system is using a different version of the
LOINC tables.

Data in this field should not be modified by the user and is generally
hidden from most data entry mechanisms.
13.25Origin Of Result (origin_of_result-63_46) ENUMERATION When this field is populated, it indicates that the accession was resulted
by an outside laboratory or non-CHCS system. The test(s) on this accession
are in the AU subscript.
 PERFORMING LABORATORY; COPATH; DBSS; OFFBOARD
13.26Verify Alert (verify_alert-63_46) ENUMERATION When this field is populated, it indicates the results from an outside
laboratory have not been verified by the submitting lab. This field is in
the AU subscript.
 RESTRICTED
13.27Staff Pathologist (staff_pathologist-63_46) POINTERThis multiple contains attributes for the name of
the staff pathologist who signed out this case.
13.28Enter Person (enter_person-63_46) POINTER (User-3)This is the ID of the user that entered the result. This
could be the transcriptionist or pathologist. It may or
may not be the same user that certifies the result. This
field will be set when the first user enters the first
uncertified result.
13.29Enter Date/Time (enter_date_time-63_46) DATE-TIMEThis field will store the date/time the results were first entered.
13.30Initial Viewer (initial_viewer-63_46) POINTER (User-3)This field stores the ID of the user who first looks at the
result via all result reporting options except the Daily
Cumulative or Interim reports. If the user is a lab user,
the field will not be set.
13.31Initial Viewer Date/Time (initial_viewer_date_time-63_46) DATE-TIMEThis field stores the date/time the result was first viewed.
13.32Rnr Hcp (rnr_hcp-63_46) POINTER (Provider-6)This field will store the ID of the Health Care Provider
or surrogate that printed, tossed, saved, or discarded the
result in Review New Results option.

15.10Cytology Non-Gyn Loinc Code (cytology_nongyn_loinc_code-63_727) STRINGThis field is the LOINC Code assigned by the system for this test result.
If the system can determine the LOINC code, it is automatically assigned.
For Autopsy, Bone Marrow, Cytology GYN, Cytology Non-GYN, and Surgical
Pathology accessions, a single LOINC code is assigned for each accession.
This LOINC code applies to all result entry fields for that accession.

Data in this field is the actual LOINC code value determined for this test.
The data is the same as the .01 field of the LOINC Codes file (file #8199).
Note this field is NOT a pointer field. This is to allow test results and
LOINC codes to be assigned that may not be in the LOINC codes file. A LOINC
code which is not in CHCS may be captured from an off-board system via an
HL-7 message when the off-board system is using a different version of the
LOINC tables.

Data in this field should not be modified by the user and is generally
hidden from most data entry mechanisms.
15.11Origin Of Result (origin_of_result-63_727) ENUMERATION When this field is populated, it indicates that the accession was resulted
by an outside laboratory or non-CHCS system. The test(s) on this accession
are in the CN subscript.
 PERFORMING LABORATORY; COPATH; DBSS; OFFBOARD
15.12Verify Alert (verify_alert-63_727) ENUMERATION When this field is populated, it indicates the results from an outside
laboratory have not been verified by the submitting lab. This field is in
the CN subscript.
 RESTRICTED
15.13Enter Person (enter_person-63_727) POINTER (User-3)This field indicates the person who entered and filed the
result. It may or may not be the same user that certifies
the result. Only lab users will see the result at this
point, as it is filed but not certified.
15.14Enter Date/Time (enter_date_time-63_727) DATE-TIMEThis field contains the date and time the result was entered
and filed. Only lab users will see the result at this point,
as it is filed but not certified.
15.15Initial Viewer (initial_viewer-63_727) POINTER (User-3)This field stores the ID of the user who first looks at
the result via all result reporting options except the
Daily Cumulative or Interim reports. If the user is a
lab user the field will not be set.
15.16Initial Viewer Date/Time (initial_viewer_date_time-63_727) DATE-TIMEThis field stores the date/time a user first viewed the result.
15.17Rnr Hcp (rnr_hcp-63_727) POINTER (Provider-6)This field will store the ID of the Health Care Provider
or surrogate that printed, tossed, saved, or discarded
a result in Review New Results option.
15.18Rnr Date/Time (rnr_date_time-63_727) DATE-TIMEThis field stores the date/time that the Health Care
Provider or surrogate tossed, printed, saved, or
discarded a result in Review New Results option.
15.19Rnr Action (rnr_action-63_727) ENUMERATION If this field contains a "1", the Health Care Provider
or surrogate discarded the result without first viewing
in Review New Results option. This field will be set
"0" if the Health Care Provider or surrogate tossed,
saved, or printed the result in Review New Results option.
 INITIALED; DISCARDED

parasite. If the entry is not included in the file,

17.12.12Enter Person (enter_person-63_737) POINTER (User-3)This field indicates the person who entered and
filed the result. It may or may not be the same
user that certifies the result. Only lab users
will see the result at this point, as it is filed
but not certified.
17.12.13Certify Date/Time (certify_date_time-63_737) DATE-TIMEThis field indicates the date and the time the result was
certified. At this point, the result becomes available to
personnel and providers outside of the laboratory.
17.12.14Certify Person (certify_person-63_737) POINTER (User-3)This field indicates what person certified the result. At this
point, the result becomes available to personnel and providers
outside of the laboratory.
17.12.15Sterility Control (sterility_control-63_737) STRINGThis is a word-processing field for entering sterility
control results. These fields are used when the lab is
entering results for the sterility controls for autoclaves.
17.12.16Sterility Result (sterility_result-63_737) STRINGThis is a word-processing field for entering
sterility culture results.

Any culture with an organism entered will automatically
be designated as an abnormal result.
 ALERT

17.12.19Initial Viewer (initial_viewer-63_737) POINTER (User-3)This field stores the ID of the user who first views the lab
result outside of the lab. This audit trail is not set when
the Daily Cumulative or Interim reports are run. This audit
trail is not set if the user has the LRLAB security key.

with the specimen. It is generated by Order Entry at

or surrogate discarded the result without first viewing
in Review New Results option. This field will be set
"0" if the Health Care Provider or surrogate tossed,
saved, or printed the result in Review New Results option.
 INITIALED; DISCARDED

outside of the laboratory.
17.12.25Organism (organism-63_737) [OBJECT] This field contians the name of the organism identified. It points to the
Etiology Field file and has a screen so the user can only select bacteria
or fungus as a result. If a bacterium is not available then have the lab
manager check the Etiology Field file for the entry. If the entry exists
in the file, then the identifier must be either a bacterium or a fungus.
If the entry is not included in the file, the lab manager may add it. Make
sure the identifier is either bacterium or fungus.
 
Subclass: Organism (63_786)
OrderLabelTypeDescription
17.12.25.1Organism (organism-63_786) POINTER (Etiology_Field-61_2)Thid field contains the name of the organism identified. It points to the
Etiology Field file and has a screen so the user can only select bacteria
or fungus as a result. If a bacterium is not available then have the lab
manager check the Etiology Field file for the entry. If the entry exists
in the file then the identifier must be either a bacterium or a fungus.
If the entry is not included in the file, the lab manager may add it. Make
sure the identifier is either bacterium or fungus.
17.12.25.2Quantity (quantity-63_786) STRINGThis field is used to quantify the amount of organism isolated. Examples: 1+, 2+, 3+, or >100,000 colonies/ml.
17.12.25.3Sic (sic-63_786) STRINGThis field contains the Serum Inhibitory Concentration of the antibiotic.
This is the concentration at which the antibiotic will kill the organism.
17.12.25.4Sbc (sbc-63_786) STRINGThis field contains the Serum Bactericidal Concentration of the antibiotic.
This is the concentration at which the antibiotic will kill the organism.
17.12.25.5Microorganism Loinc Code (microorganism_loinc_code-63_786) STRINGThis field is the LOINC Code assigned by the system for this test result.
If the system can determine the LOINC code, it is automatically assigned.
For Bacteriology accessions, a LOINC Code is captured for the GRAM STAIN
field (if this field is populated during result entry), for each
microorganism identified, and for each antibiotic tested. Data in this
field is the actual LOINC code value determined for this test. The data is
the same as the .01 field of the LOINC Codes file (file #8199). Note this
field is NOT a pointer field. This is to allow test results and LOINC codes
to be assigned that may not be in the LOINC codes file. A LOINC code which
is not in CHCS may be captured from an off-board system via an HL-7 message
when the off-board system is using a different version of the LOINC tables.

Data in this field should not be modified by the user and is generally
hidden from most data entry mechanisms.
17.12.25.6Bt Org Snomed Ct (bt_org_snomed_ct-63_786) STRINGThis field contains the SNOMED CT codes generated from the Etiology file.

19.12.8Fungus/Yeast (fungus_yeast-63_753) [OBJECT] This is a multiple field which contains attributes

not included in the file, the lab manager may add it.

OrderLabelTypeDescription

19.12.8.3Fungus/Yeast Loinc Code (fungus_yeast_loinc_code-63_755) STRINGThis field is the LOINC Code assigned by the system for this test result.
If the system can determine the LOINC code, it is automatically assigned.
For Mycology accessions, a LOINC code is captured for each Fungus/Yeast
identified.

Data in this field is the actual LOINC code value determined for this test.
The data is the same as the .01 field of the LOINC Codes file (file #8199).
Note this field is NOT a pointer field. This is to allow test results and
LOINC codes to be assigned that may not be in the LOINC codes file. A LOINC
code which is not in CHCS may be captured from an off-board system via an
HL-7 message when the off-board system is using a different version of the
LOINC tables.

Data in this field should not be modified by the user and is generally
hidden from most data entry mechanisms.

EX: 1234 reversed is 34^12) \r     test = process test, pointer to #60\r     TYPE = IN or OUT patient flag I=in, O=out \r \rSpecial technical information regarding all fields that contain the\rword LOINC in their field name. The acronym LOINC is for (L)ogical\r(O)bservation (I)dentifiers, (N)ames, and (C)odes.\r \rThe various LOINC Code fields are the actual LOINC Code assigned by the\rsystem for a test result. If the system can determine the LOINC code, it is\rautomatically assigned. For Clinical Chemistry tests, LOINC codes are\rderived by the system based on the component name of the test, the\rsite/specimen for the accession, and lab method used during result entry.\rThe Lab Method contains the necessary references to determine the\rappropriate LOINC Time Aspect, LOINC Property, LOINC System/Sample (which\ris further linked via the Topography Field file), LOINC Scale, and\roptionally LOINC Method. For Bacteriology accessions, a LOINC Code is\rcaptured for the GRAM STAIN field (if this field is populated during result\rentry), for each microorganism identified, and for each antibiotic tested.\rFor Autopsy, Bone Marrow, Cytology GYN, Cytology Non-GYN, and Surgical\rPathology accessions, a single LOINC code is assigned for each accession.\rThis LOINC code applies to all result entry fields for that accession. For\rMycology accessions, a LOINC code is captured for each Fungus/Yeast\ridentified. For Parasitology, a LOINC code is captured for each parasite\ridentified. For Mycobacterium, LOINC codes are captured for each\rMycobacterium identified and each antibiotic tested. For Virology, a LOINC\rcode is captured for each virus identified.\r \rTests in the BB (Blood Bank) subscript currently are not assigned LOINC\rcodes. CHCS is not considered the source of blood bank test results, the\rDBSS (Defense Blood Standard System) is the source. LOINC Codes should be\rderived on the system that is the source of the test results. At this time\r(March 1999), the DBSS system and the HL-7 interface between CHCS and DBSS\rdoes not support the exchange of LOINC codes for Blood Bank test results,\rantibody identifications, or blood product management.\r \rData in these fields are actual LOINC code values determined by the system\rfor a particular test result. The data have the same values as the .01\rfield of the LOINC Codes file (file #8199). Note these fields are NOT\rpointer fields. This is to allow test results and LOINC codes to be\rassigned that may not be in the LOINC codes file. A LOINC code which is not\rin CHCS may be captured from an off-board system via an HL-7 message when\rthe off-board system is using a different version of the LOINC tables.\r \rData in these fields should not be modified by the user and are generally\rhidden from most data entry mechanisms. Only authorized support personnel\rshould change data in the LOINC code fields.",
